TOOLKIT & METHODOLOGY\n\n## 3.1 TOOL SELECTION PRINCIPLES\n\n- IMAGE TOOL PRIORITY:\n  * For any request involving image creation, modification, style change, or visual design, ALWAYS prefer the Image Tool.\n  * Do NOT describe images purely in text when an image output is expected.\n  * If an image result is required, the Image Tool is mandatory.\n\n- CLI TOOLS PREFERENCE:\n  * Always prefer CLI tools over Python scripts when possible\n  * CLI tools are generally faster and more efficient for:\n    1. Synchronous Commands (blocking):\n      * You can omit `blocking`, as it defaults to true\n      * Use for quick operations that complete within 60 seconds\n      * Commands run directly and wait for completion\n      * Example:\n        <function_calls>\n        <execute-command session_name="default" blocking="true">\n        ls -l\n        </execute-command>\n        </function_calls>\n        (or simply omit the blocking parameter as it defaults to true)\n      * IMPORTANT: Do not use for long-running operations as they will timeout after 60 seconds\n\n  2. Asynchronous Commands (non-blocking):\n      * Use `blocking="false"` for any command that might take longer than 60 seconds or for starting background services\n      * Commands run in background and return immediately\n      * Example:\n        <function_calls>\n        <execute-command session_name="dev" blocking="false">\n        npm run dev\n        </execute-command>\n        </function_calls>\n      * Common use cases:\n        - Development servers (Next.js, React, etc.)\n        - Build processes\n        - Long-running data processing\n        - Background services\n\n- Session Management:\n  * Each command must specify a session_name\n  * Use consistent session names for related commands\n  * Different sessions are isolated from each other\n  * Example: Use "build" session for build commands, "dev" for development servers\n  * Sessions maintain state between commands\n\n- Command Execution Guidelines:\n  * For commands that might take longer than 60 seconds, ALWAYS use run_async="true"\n  * Do not rely on increasing timeout for long-running commands\n  * Use proper session names for organization\n  * Chain commands with && for sequential execution\n  * Use | for piping output between commands\n  * Redirect output to files for long-running processes\n\n- Avoid commands requiring confirmation; actively use -y or -f flags for automatic confirmation\n- Avoid commands with excessive output; save to files when necessary\n- Chain multiple commands with operators to minimize interruptions and improve efficiency:\n  1. Use && for sequential execution: `command1 && command2 && command3`\n  2. Use || for fallback execution: `command1 || command2`\n  3. Use ; for unconditional execution: `command1; command2`\n  4. Use | for piping output: `command1 | command2`\n  5. Use > and >> for output redirection: `command > file` or `command >> file`\n- Use pipe operator to pass command outputs, simplifying operations\n- Use non-interactive `bc` for simple calculations, Python for complex math; never calculate mentally\n- Use `uptime` command when users explicitly request sandbox status check or wake-up\n\n## 3.3 CODE DEVELOPMENT PRACTICES\n- CODING:\n  * Must save code to files before execution; direct code input to interpreter commands is forbidden\n  * Write Python code for complex mathematical calculations and analysis\n  * Use search tools to find solutions when encountering unfamiliar problems\n  * For index.html, use deployment tools directly, or package everything into a zip file and provide it as a message attachment\n  * When creating web interfaces, always create CSS files first before HTML to ensure proper styling and design consistency\n  * For images, use real image URLs from sources like unsplash.com, pexels.com, pixabay.com, giphy.com, or wikimedia.org instead of creating placeholder images; use placeholder.com only as a last resort\n\n- WEBSITE DEPLOYMENT:\n  * Only use the \'deploy\' tool when users explicitly request permanent deployment to a production environment\n  * The deploy tool publishes static HTML+CSS+JS sites to a public URL using S3 web Pages\n  * If the same name is used for deployment, it will redeploy to the same project as before\n  * For temporary or development purposes, serve files locally instead of using the deployment tool\n  * When editing HTML files, always share the preview URL provided by the automatically running HTTP server with the user\n  * The preview URL is automatically generated and available in the tool results when creating or editing HTML files\n  * When deploying, ensure all assets (images, scripts, stylesheets) use relative paths to work correctly\n\n- PYTHON EXECUTION: Create reusable modules with proper error handling and logging. Use for precise text matching\n  2. Combine with CLI tools for powerful searches\n  3. Save complex patterns to files for reuse\n  4. Test patterns with small samples first\n  5. Use extended regex (-E) for complex patterns\n- Data Processing Workflow:\n  1. Use grep to locate relevant files\n  2. Use head/tail to preview content\n  3. Use awk for data extraction\n  4. WORKFLOW MANAGEMENT\n\n## 5.1 AUTONOMOUS WORKFLOW SYSTEM\nYou operate through a self-maintained todo.md file that serves as your central source of truth and execution roadmap:\n\n1. Upon receiving a task, immediately create a lean, focused todo.md with essential sections covering the task lifecycle\n2. Each section contains specific, actionable subtasks based on complexity - use only as many as needed, no more\n3. Each task should be specific, actionable, and have clear completion criteria\n4. MUST actively work through these tasks one by one, checking them off as completed\n5. Adapt the plan as needed while maintaining its integrity as your execution compass\n\n## 5.2 TODO.MD FILE STRUCTURE AND USAGE\nThe todo.md file is your primary working document and action plan:\n\n1. Contains the complete list of tasks you MUST complete to fulfill the user\'s request\n2. Format with clear sections, each containing specific tasks marked with [ ] (incomplete) or [x] (complete)\n3. Each task should be specific, actionable, and have clear completion criteria\n4. MUST actively work through these tasks one by one, checking them off as completed\n5. Before every action, consult your todo.md to determine which task to tackle next\n6. The todo.md serves as your instruction set - if a task is in todo.md, you are responsible for completing it\n7. Update the todo.md as you make progress, adding new tasks as needed and marking completed ones\n8. Never delete tasks from todo.md - instead mark them complete with [x] to maintain a record of your work\n9. Once ALL tasks in todo.md are marked complete [x], you MUST call either the \'complete\' state or \'ask\' tool to signal task completion\n10. SCOPE CONSTRAINT: Focus on completing existing tasks before adding new ones; avoid continuously expanding scope\n11. CAPABILITY AWARENESS: Only add tasks that are achievable with your available tools and capabilities\n12. FINALITY: After marking a section complete, do not reopen it or add new tasks unless explicitly directed by the user\n13. STOPPING CONDITION: If you\'ve made 3 consecutive updates to todo.md without completing any tasks, reassess your approach and either simplify your plan or **use the \'ask\' tool to seek user guidance.**\n14. COMPLETION VERIFICATION: Only mark a task as [x] complete when you have concrete evidence of completion\n15. SIMPLICITY: Keep your todo.md lean and direct with clear actions, avoiding unnecessary verbosity or granularity\n\n## 5.3 EXECUTION PHILOSOPHY\nYour approach is deliberately methodical and persistent:\n\n1. Operate in a continuous loop until explicitly stopped\n2. Execute one step at a time, following a consistent loop: evaluate state → select tool → execute → provide narrative update → track progress\n3. Every action is guided by your todo.md, consulting it before selecting any tool\n4. Thoroughly verify each completed step before moving forward\n5. **Provide Markdown-formatted narrative updates directly in your responses** to keep the user informed of your progress, explain your thinking, and clarify the next steps. Use headers, brief descriptions, and context to make your process transparent.\n6. CRITICALLY IMPORTANT: Continue running in a loop until either:\n  - Using the **\'ask\' tool (THE ONLY TOOL THE USER CAN RESPOND TO)** to wait for essential user input (this pauses the loop)\n  - Using the \'complete\' tool when ALL tasks are finished\n7. For casual conversation:\n  - Use **\'ask\'** to properly end the conversation and wait for user input (**USER CAN RESPOND**)\n8. For tasks:\n  - Use **\'ask\'** when you need essential user input to proceed (**USER CAN RESPOND**)\n  - Provide **narrative updates** frequently in your responses to keep the user informed without requiring their input\n  - Use \'complete\' only when ALL tasks are finished\n9. MANDATORY COMPLETION:\n  - IMMEDIATELY use \'complete\' or \'ask\' after ALL tasks in todo.md are marked [x]\n  - NO additional commands or verifications after all tasks are complete\n  - NO further exploration or information gathering after completion\n  - NO redundant checks or validations after completion\n  - FAILURE to use \'complete\' or \'ask\' after task completion is a critical error\n\n## 5.4 TASK MANAGEMENT CYCLE\n1. STATE EVALUATION: Examine Todo.md for priorities, analyze recent Tool Results for environment understanding, and review past actions for context\n2. TOOL SELECTION: Choose exactly one tool that advances the current todo item\n3. EXECUTION: Wait for tool execution and observe results\n4. **NARRATIVE UPDATE:** Provide a **Markdown-formatted** narrative update directly in your response before the next tool call. Include explanations of what you\'ve done, what you\'re about to do, and why. Use headers, brief paragraphs, and formatting to enhance readability.\n5. PROGRESS TRACKING: Update todo.md with completed items and new tasks\n6. METHODICAL ITERATION: Repeat until section completion\n7. SECTION TRANSITION: Document completion and move to next section\n8. COMPLETION: IMMEDIATELY use \'complete\' or \'ask\' when ALL tasks are finished\n\n# 6. CONTENT CREATION\n\n## 6.1 WRITING GUIDELINES\n- Write content in continuous paragraphs using varied sentence lengths for engaging prose; avoid list formatting\n- Use prose and paragraphs by default; provide detailed content with proper citations\n- Strictly follow requirements in writing rules, and avoid using list formats in any files except todo.md\n\n## 6.2 DESIGN GUIDELINES\n- For any design-related task, first create the design in HTML+CSS to ensure maximum flexibility\n- Designs should be created with print-friendliness in mind - use appropriate margins, page breaks, and printable color schemes\n- After creating designs in HTML+CSS, convert directly to PDF as the final output format\n- When designing multi-page documents, ensure consistent styling and proper page numbering\n- Test print-readiness by confirming designs display correctly in print preview mode\n- For complex designs, test different media queries including print media type\n- Package all design assets (HTML, CSS, images, and PDF output) together when delivering final results\n- Ensure all fonts are properly embedded or use web-safe fonts to maintain design integrity in the PDF output\n- Set appropriate page sizes (A4, Letter, etc.) in the CSS using @page rules for consistent PDF rendering\n\n## Image Guidelines\n- ALWAYS use the Image Tool for image generation or image editing tasks\n- Write a single self-contained image prompt before calling the Image Tool\n- Clearly describe the main subject and overall composition\n- Explicitly specify the intended visual style and aesthetic\n- Provide exact text content if text is required; Deepfake Detection and Content Authentication Module\n//!\n//! This module provides comprehensive deepfake detection capabilities including:\n//! - Media analysis for video, audio, and image content\n//! - Content authentication through watermarking and digital signatures\n//! - Threat intelligence integration for known deepfake patterns\n//! - Real-time detection pipelines for streaming media\n\npub mod analysis;\npub mod authentication;\npub mod detection;\npub mod threat_intel;\npub mod models;\n\nuse anyhow::Result;\nuse async_trait::async_trait;\nuse chrono::{DateTime, Utc};\nuse serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};\nuse std::collections::HashMap;\nuse std::sync::Arc;\nuse tokio::sync::RwLock;\nuse tracing::{debug, error, info, warn};\nuse uuid::Uuid;\n\npub use analysis::{MediaAnalyzer, AnalysisResult, AnalysisType};\npub use authentication::{ContentAuthenticator, AuthenticationResult, WatermarkConfig};\npub use detection::{DeepfakeDetector, DetectionResult, DetectionConfig};\npub use threat_intel::{ThreatIntelIntegration, ThreatInfo, ThreatMatch};\npub use models::{MediaContent, MediaType, DeepfakeType, ConfidenceLevel};\n\n/// Main manager for deepfake detection operations\npub struct DeepfakeManager {\n    /// Media analyzer for content analysis\n    analyzer: Arc<RwLock<MediaAnalyzer>>,\n    /// Deepfake detector for identifying manipulated content\n    detector: Arc<RwLock<DeepfakeDetector>>,\n    /// Content authenticator for watermarking and signatures\n    authenticator: Arc<RwLock<ContentAuthenticator>>,\n    /// Threat intelligence integration\n    threat_intel: Arc<RwLock<ThreatIntelIntegration>>,\n    /// Configuration\n    config: DeepfakeConfig,\n    /// Detection statistics\n    stats: Arc<RwLock<DetectionStats>>,\n}\n\n/// Configuration for the deepfake detection system\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct DeepfakeConfig {\n    /// Enable real-time detection\n    pub real_time_detection: bool,\n    /// Minimum confidence threshold for alerts\n    pub alert_threshold: f32,\n    /// Enable automatic content authentication\n    pub auto_authenticate: bool,\n    /// Enable threat intelligence lookup\n    pub threat_intel_enabled: bool,\n    /// Maximum media size in bytes (default: 500MB)\n    pub max_media_size: usize,\n    /// Analysis timeout in seconds\n    pub analysis_timeout: u64,\n    /// Enable detailed logging\n    pub detailed_logging: bool,\n}\n\nimpl Default for DeepfakeConfig {\n    fn default() -> Self {\n        Self {\n            real_time_detection: true,\n            alert_threshold: 0.75,\n            auto_authenticate: true,\n            threat_intel_enabled: true,\n            max_media_size: 500 * 1024 * 1024, // 500MB\n            analysis_timeout: 300, // 5 minutes\n            detailed_logging: false,\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Statistics for detection operations\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Default, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct DetectionStats {\n    /// Total media analyzed\n    pub total_analyzed: u64,\n    /// Deepfakes detected\n    pub deepfakes_detected: u64,\n    /// False positives reported\n    pub false_positives: u64,\n    /// Average analysis time in milliseconds\n    pub avg_analysis_time_ms: f64,\n    /// By media type breakdown\n    pub by_media_type: HashMap<String, u64>,\n    /// By deepfake type breakdown\n    pub by_deepfake_type: HashMap<String, u64>,\n}\n\nimpl DeepfakeManager {\n    /// Create a new DeepfakeManager with the given configuration\n    pub fn new(config: DeepfakeConfig) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            analyzer: Arc::new(RwLock::new(MediaAnalyzer::new())),\n            detector: Arc::new(RwLock::new(DeepfakeDetector::new(DetectionConfig::default()))),\n            authenticator: Arc::new(RwLock::new(ContentAuthenticator::new())),\n            threat_intel: Arc::new(RwLock::new(ThreatIntelIntegration::new())),\n            config,\n            stats: Arc::new(RwLock::new(DetectionStats::default())),\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Analyze media content for deepfake detection\n    pub async fn analyze_media(&self, media: &MediaContent) -> Result<DeepfakeAnalysisResult> {\n        let start_time = std::time::Instant::now();\n        let mut stats = self.stats.write().await;\n\n        // Validate media size\n        if media.data.len() > self.config.max_media_size {\n            return Err(anyhow::anyhow!(\n                "Media size exceeds maximum allowed: {} > {}",\n                media.data.len(),\n                self.config.max_media_size\n            ));\n        }\n\n        info!("Analyzing media: {} ({:?})", media.id, media.media_type);\n\n        // Step 1: Run media analysis\n        let analyzer = self.analyzer.read().await;\n        let analysis_result = analyzer.analyze(media).await?;\n        drop(analyzer);\n\n        // Step 2: Run deepfake detection\n        let detector = self.detector.read().await;\n        let detection_result = detector.detect(media, &analysis_result).await?;\n        drop(detector);\n\n        // Step 3: Check threat intelligence\n        let threat_matches = if self.config.threat_intel_enabled {\n            let threat_intel = self.threat_intel.read().await;\n            threat_intel.lookup(media).await?\n        } else {\n            vec![]\n        };\n\n        // Step 4: Calculate final result\n        let is_deepfake = detection_result.is_deepfake;\n        let confidence = detection_result.confidence;\n        \n        // Update statistics\n        stats.total_analyzed += 1;\n        if is_deepfake {\n            stats.deepfakes_detected += 1;\n        }\n        *stats.by_media_type.entry(media.media_type.to_string()).or_insert(0) += 1;\n        if is_deepfake {\n            for df_type in &detection_result.deepfake_types {\n                *stats.by_deepfake_type.entry(df_type.to_string()).or_insert(0) += 1;\n            }\n        }\n        \n        let elapsed = start_time.elapsed();\n        stats.avg_analysis_time_ms = \n            (stats.avg_analysis_time_ms * (stats.total_analyzed - 1) as f64 + elapsed.as_millis() as f64)\n            / stats.total_analyzed as f64;\n\n        // Generate alert if threshold exceeded\n        if is_deepfake && confidence >= self.config.alert_threshold {\n            warn!(\n                "Deepfake detected! Confidence: {:.2}%, Types: {:?}",\n                confidence * 100.0,\n                detection_result.deepfake_types\n            );\n        }\n\n        Ok(DeepfakeAnalysisResult {\n            media_id: media.id.clone(),\n            is_deepfake,\n            confidence,\n            deepfake_types: detection_result.deepfake_types,\n            analysis_result,\n            detection_details: detection_result.details,\n            threat_matches,\n            recommendations: self.generate_recommendations(is_deepfake, confidence),\n            timestamp: Utc::now(),\n        })\n    }\n\n    /// Authenticate content by adding watermarks and signatures\n    pub async fn authenticate_content(\n        &self,\n        media: &mut MediaContent,\n        config: Option<WatermarkConfig>,\n    ) -> Result<AuthenticationResult> {\n        let authenticator = self.authenticator.read().await;\n        let result = authenticator.authenticate(media, config).await?;\n        \n        // Update media with authentication info\n        media.authenticated = true;\n        media.authentication_id = Some(result.authentication_id.clone());\n        \n        info!("Content authenticated: {}", result.authentication_id);\n        Ok(result)\n    }\n\n    /// Verify content authentication\n    pub async fn verify_authentication(&self, media: &MediaContent) -> Result<VerificationResult> {\n        let authenticator = self.authenticator.read().await;\n        authenticator.verify(media).await\n    }\n\n    /// Get detection statistics\n    pub async fn get_stats(&self) -> DetectionStats {\n        self.stats.read().await.clone()\n    }\n\n    /// Generate recommendations based on detection results\n    fn generate_recommendations(&self, is_deepfake: bool, confidence: f32) -> Vec<String> {\n        let mut recommendations = Vec::new();\n\n        if is_deepfake {\n            if confidence >= 0.9 {\n                recommendations.push("HIGH CONFIDENCE: Content is likely a deepfake. Do not distribute.".to_string());\n                recommendations.push("Report to content moderation team immediately.".to_string());\n            } else if confidence >= 0.75 {\n                recommendations.push("LIKELY DEEPFAKE: Manual review recommended before distribution.".to_string());\n            } else {\n                recommendations.push("SUSPICIOUS: Additional verification recommended.".to_string());\n            }\n            \n            recommendations.push("Consider using reverse image search to find original content.".to_string());\n            recommendations.push("Check metadata and source credibility.".to_string());\n        } else {\n            recommendations.push("Content appears authentic based on analysis.".to_string());\n            if confidence < 0.5 {\n                recommendations.push("Note: Low confidence detection. Consider additional analysis.".to_string());\n            }\n        }\n\n        recommendations\n    }\n\n    /// Add custom detection model\n    pub async fn add_detection_model(&self, model: DetectionModel) -> Result<()> {\n        let mut detector = self.detector.write().await;\n        detector.add_model(model).await\n    }\n\n    /// Update threat intelligence feed\n    pub async fn update_threat_intel(&self) -> Result<()> {\n        let mut threat_intel = self.threat_intel.write().await;\n        threat_intel.update_feeds().await\n    }\n}\n\n/// Result of deepfake analysis\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct DeepfakeAnalysisResult {\n    /// Media identifier\n    pub media_id: String,\n    /// Whether content is detected as deepfake\n    pub is_deepfake: bool,\n    /// Detection confidence (0.0 - 1.0)\n    pub confidence: f32,\n    /// Types of deepfakes detected\n    pub deepfake_types: Vec<DeepfakeType>,\n    /// Detailed analysis result\n    pub analysis_result: AnalysisResult,\n    /// Detection details\n    pub detection_details: String,\n    /// Threat intelligence matches\n    pub threat_matches: Vec<ThreatMatch>,\n    /// Recommendations for action\n    pub recommendations: Vec<String>,\n    /// Analysis timestamp\n    pub timestamp: DateTime<Utc>,\n}\n\n/// Result of authentication verification\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct VerificationResult {\n    /// Whether content is verified authentic\n    pub verified: bool,\n    /// Authentication ID if present\n    pub authentication_id: Option<String>,\n    /// Verification confidence\n    pub confidence: f32,\n    /// Watermark intact\n    pub watermark_intact: bool,\n    /// Signature valid\n    pub signature_valid: bool,\n    /// Timestamp of verification\n    pub timestamp: DateTime<Utc>,\n}\n\n/// Detection model configuration\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct DetectionModel {\n    /// Model identifier\n    pub id: String,\n    /// Model name\n    pub name: String,\n    /// Model version\n    pub version: String,\n    /// Model type (e.g., "neural", "statistical", "hybrid")\n    pub model_type: String,\n    /// Target deepfake types\n    pub target_types: Vec<DeepfakeType>,\n    /// Detection accuracy (0.0 - 1.0)\n    pub accuracy: f32,\n    /// Model weights/binary path\n    pub model_path: Option<String>,\n    /// Whether model is active\n    pub active: bool,\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn test_deepfake_manager_creation() {\n        let manager = DeepfakeManager::new(DeepfakeConfig::default());\n        let stats = manager.get_stats().await;\n        assert_eq!(stats.total_analyzed, 0);\n    }\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn test_stats_update() {\n        let manager = DeepfakeManager::new(DeepfakeConfig::default());\n        \n        // Create test media\n        let media = MediaContent {\n            id: Uuid::new_v4().to_string(),\n            media_type: MediaType::Image,\n            data: vec![0u8; 1000],\n            metadata: HashMap::new(),\n            authenticated: false,\n            authentication_id: None,\n            created_at: Utc::now(),\n        };\n\n        let result = manager.analyze_media(&media).await;\n        assert!(result.is_ok());\n        \n        let stats = manager.get_stats().await;\n        assert_eq!(stats.total_analyzed, 1);\n    }\n}\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

-> Self {\n        self.metadata.insert(key.to_string(), value.to_string());\n        self\n    }\n\n    /// Get file extension based on media type\n    pub fn extension(&self) -> &str {\n        self.metadata.get("extension").map(|s| s.as_str()).unwrap_or_else(|| {\n            match self.media_type {\n                MediaType::Image => "jpg",\n                MediaType::Video => "mp4",\n                MediaType::Audio => "mp3",\n            }\n        })\n    }\n}\n\n/// Type of media content\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Hash, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n#[serde(rename_all = "snake_case")]\npub enum MediaType {\n    /// Image content (JPEG, PNG, etc.)\n    Image,\n    /// Video content (MP4, AVI, etc.)\n    Video,\n    /// Audio content (MP3, WAV, etc.)\n    Audio,\n}\n\nimpl std::fmt::Display for MediaType {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<\'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {\n        match self {\n            MediaType::Image => write!(f, "Attribution possible - related to: {}",\n                pattern.actors.join(", ")\n            ));\n        }\n\n        recommendations\n    }\n\n    /// Calculate content hash\n    fn calculate_hash(&self, data: &[u8]) -> String {\n        use sha2::{Digest, Sha256};\n        let mut hasher = Sha256::new();\n        hasher.update(data);\n        let hash = hasher.finalize();\n        hex::encode(hash)\n    }\n\n    /// Update threat intelligence feeds\n    pub async fn update_feeds(&mut self) -> Result<()> {\n        info!("Updating threat intelligence feeds");\n\n        for feed in &mut self.feeds {\n            if !feed.active {\n                continue;\n            }\n\n            // Simulate feed update\n            feed.last_update = Some(Utc::now());\n            debug!("Updated feed: {} ({})", feed.name, feed.id);\n        }\n\n        let mut stats = self.stats.write().await;\n        stats.feed_updates += 1;\n        stats.last_update = Some(Utc::now());\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Add threat to database\n    pub async fn add_threat(&self, info: ThreatInfo, content_hash: &str) -> Result<()> {\n        let mut hash_db = self.hash_database.write().await;\n        hash_db.insert(content_hash.to_string(), info);\n\n        let mut stats = self.stats.write().await;\n        stats.unique_threats += 1;\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Get threat patterns\n    pub async fn get_patterns(&self) -> Vec<ThreatPattern> {\n        self.patterns.read().await.clone()\n    }\n\n    /// Get threat actors\n    pub async fn get_actors(&self) -> Vec<ThreatActor> {\n        self.actors.read().await.clone()\n    }\n\n    /// Get campaigns\n    pub async fn get_campaigns(&self) -> Vec<Campaign> {\n        self.campaigns.read().await.clone()\n    }\n\n    /// Get statistics\n    pub async fn get_stats(&self) -> ThreatIntelStats {\n        self.stats.read().await.clone()\n    }\n\n    /// Add custom threat pattern\n    pub async fn add_pattern(&self, pattern: ThreatPattern) -> Result<()> {\n        let mut patterns = self.patterns.write().await;\n        patterns.push(pattern);\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Add threat actor\n    pub async fn add_actor(&self, actor: ThreatActor) -> Result<()> {\n        let mut actors = self.actors.write().await;\n        actors.push(actor);\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Add campaign\n    pub async fn add_campaign(&self, campaign: Campaign) -> Result<()> {\n        let mut campaigns = self.campaigns.write().await;\n        campaigns.push(campaign);\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n\nimpl Default for ThreatIntelIntegration {\n    fn default() -> Self {\n        Self::new()\n    }\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use Comprehensive security for AI/ML systems including:\n//! - AI Data Security: Pipeline controls, data encryption, access management\n//! - AI Model Security: Model encryption, watermarking, integrity verification\n//! - AI API Security: Prompt injection detection, input validation, rate limiting\n//! - MLOps Security: Pipeline security, model registry, deployment controls\n\npub mod   /// Security level (1-10)\n    pub security_level: u8,\n}\n\nimpl Default for AISecurityConfig {\n    fn default() -> Self {\n        Self {\n            data_encryption_enabled: true,\n            model_watermarking_enabled: true,\n            prompt_injection_detection: true,\n            input_validation: true,\n            audit_logging: true,\n            max_input_size: 100 * 1024, // detected\n    pub prompt_injections_detected: u64,\n    /// Data breaches prevented\n    pub data_breaches_prevented: u64,\n    /// Models protected\n    pub models_protected: u64,\n    /// Security events\n    pub security_events: u64,\n}\n\nimpl AISecurityManager {\n    /// Create a new AI Security Manager\n    pub fn new(config: AISecurityConfig) -> Self {\n        Self {\n std::time::Instant::now();\n\n        // Step 1: Secure data pipelines\n        let data_result = self.secure_data_pipelines(system).await?;\n\n        // Step 2: Secure models\n        let model_result = self.secure_models(system).await?;\n\n        // Step 3: Configure API security\n        let api_result = self.configure_api_security(system).await?;\n\n        // Step 4: Setup MLOps security\n        let mlops_result = self.setup_mlops_security(system).await?;\n\n        // Update system status\n        system.secured = true;\n        system.security_level = self.config.security_level;\n\n        let result = SecurityResult {\n            system_id: system.id.clone(),\n            data_security: data_result,\n            model_security: model_result,\n            api_security: api_result,\n            mlops_security: mlops_result,\n            overall_status: SecurityStatus::Secured,\n            applied_policies: self.get_applied_policies(system).await,\n            duration_ms: start_time.elapsed().as_millis() as u64,\n            timestamp: Utc::now(),\n        };\n\n        // Log event\n        self.log_security_event(SecurityEvent {\n            id: Uuid::new_v4().to_string(),\n            event_type: SecurityEventType::SystemSecured,\n            system_id: Some(system.id.clone()),\n            model_id: None,\n            description: format!("AI system {} secured", system.id),\n            severity: ThreatLevel::Info,\n            timestamp: Utc::now(),\n            metadata: let data_security = self.data_security.read().await;\n        \n        let mut result = DataSecurityResult::default();\n        \n        for pipeline in &system.data_pipelines {\n            let pipeline_result = data_security.secure_pipeline(pipeline).await?;\n            if pipeline_result.encrypted {\n                result.encrypted_pipelines += 1;\n            }\n            if pipeline_result.access_controlled {\n                result.access_controlled_pipelines += 1;\n            }\n            result.total_pipelines += 1;\n        }\n\n        Ok(result)\n    }\n\n    /// Secure models\n    async fn secure_models(&self, system: &AISystem) -> Result<ModelSecurityResult> {\n        let model_security = self.model_security.read().await;\n        \n        let mut result = ModelSecurityResult::default();\n        \n        for model in &system.models {\n            let model_result = model_security.protect_model(model).await?;\n            if model_result.encrypted {\n                result.encrypted_models += 1;\n            }\n            if model_result.watermarked {\n                result.watermarked_models += 1;\n            }\n            result.total_models += 1;\n        }\n\n        let mut stats = self.stats.write().await;\n        stats.models_protected += result.total_models;\n        drop(stats);\n\n        Ok(result)\n    }\n\n    /// Configure API security\n    async fn configure_api_security(&self, system: &AISystem) -> Result<APISecurityResult> {\n        let api_security = self.api_security.read().await;\n        \n        let result = APISecurityResult {\n            prompt_injection_enabled: self.config.prompt_injection_detection,\n            input_validation_enabled: self.config.input_validation,\n  pub async fn validate_input(&self, input: &str, context: &SecurityContext) -> Result<InputValidationResult> {\n        let mut stats = self.stats.write().await;\n        stats.total_requests += 1;\n        drop(stats);\n\n        // Check input size\n        if input.len() > self.config.max_input_size {\n            let mut stats = self.stats.write().await;\n            stats.blocked_requests += 1;\n            drop(stats);\n\n            return Ok(InputValidationResult {\n                valid: false,\n                reason: Some("Input exceeds maximum size".to_string()),\n                threat_level: ThreatLevel::Medium,\n                detected_threats: vec!["oversized_input".to_string()],\n                sanitized_input: None,\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Check for prompt injection\n        if self.config.prompt_injection_detection {\n            let api_security = self.api_security.read().await;\n            let injection_result = api_security.detect_prompt_injection(input).await?;\n            \n            if injection_result.detected {\n                let mut stats = self.stats.write().await;\n                stats.blocked_requests += 1;\n                stats.prompt_injections_detected += 1;\n                drop(stats);\n\n                // Log event\n                self.log_security_event(SecurityEvent {\n                    id: Uuid::new_v4().to_string(),\n                    event_type: SecurityEventType::PromptInjectionDetected,\n injection_result.attack_type)),\n                    threat_level: ThreatLevel::High,\n                    detected_threats: injection_result.indicators,\n                    sanitized_input: None,\n                });\n            }\n        }\n\n        Ok(InputValidationResult {\n            valid: true,\n            reason: None,\n            threat_level: ThreatLevel::Info,\n            detected_threats: vec![],\n            sanitized_input: Some(input.to_string()),\n        })\n    }\n\n    /// Log a security event\n    async fn log_security_event(&self, event: SecurityEvent) -> self.stats.write().await;\n            stats.security_events += 1;\n        }\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Get applied policies for a system\n    async fn get_applied_policies(&self, _system: (Permission::Execute, Permission::Execute) => true,\n            (Permission::Write, Permission::Read) => true,\n            _ => false,\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Evaluate conditions\n    fn self.stats.write().await;\n                    stats.total_detections += 1;\n                    *stats.by_type.entry(pattern.attack_type.clone()).or_insert(0) += 1;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Additional heuristic checks\n        let heuristic_result = self.heuristic_check(input);\n        if heuristic_result.suspicious {\n            detected = true;\n            indicators.extend(heuristic_result.indicators);\n        }\n\n        Ok(PromptInjectionResult {\n            detected,\n            attack_type,\n            indicators,\n            severity: max_severity,\n            confidence: if detected { 0.85 } else { 0.0 },\n        })\n    }\n\n    /// Heuristic check for injection patterns\n    fn heuristic_check(&self, input: &str) -> HeuristicResult {\n        let mut result = HeuristicResult::default();\n        \n        // Check for unusual repetition\n        let words: Vec<&str> = input.split_whitespace().collect();\n        if words.len() > 10 {\n            let unique_words: std::collections::HashSet<&str> = words.iter().copied().collect();\n            let ratio = unique_words.len() as f32 / words.len() as f32;\n            if ratio < 0.3 {\n                result.suspicious = true;\n                result.indicators.push("low_word_diversity".to_string());\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Check for unusual character patterns\n        if input.contains("{{") || input.contains("}}") {\n            result.suspicious = true;\n            result.indicators.push("template_injection".to_string());\n        }\n\n        // Check for base64 encoded content (potential obfuscation)\n        if input.len() > 50 {\n            let base64_pattern = Regex::new(r"[A-Za-z0-9+/]{20,}=*").unwrap();\n            if base64_pattern.is_match(input) {\n                result.suspicious = true;\n                result.indicators.push("potential_obfuscation".to_string());\n            }\n        }\n\n        result\n    }\n}\n\nimpl Default for PromptInjectionDetector {\n    fn default() -> Self {\n        Self::new()\n    }\n}\n\n/// Injection pattern\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct InjectionPattern {\n    /// Pattern name\n    pub name: String,\n    /// Regex pattern\n    pub pattern: String,\n    /// Attack type\n    pub attack_type: String,\n    /// Severity\n    pub severity: allowed_patterns: Vec<String>,\n}\n\nimpl InputValidator {\n    /// Create new input validator\n    pub fn new() -> Self {\n        Self {\n            max_length: 100_000,\n            allowed_patterns: vec![\n                r"[\\w\\s.,!?;:\'\\"()-]+".to_string(),\n            ],\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Validate input\n    pub async fn validate(&self, input: &str, config: &InputValidationConfig) -> Result<InputValidationResult> {\n        let mut detected_threats = Vec::new();\n\n        // Check length\n        if input.len() > config.max_input_size {\n            return Ok(InputValidationResult {\n                valid: false,\n                reason: Some(format!("Input exceeds maximum size: {} > {}", input.len(), config.max_input_size)),\n                threat_level: ThreatLevel::Medium,\n                detected_threats: vec!["oversized_input".to_string()],\n                sanitized_input: None,\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Check for null bytes\n        if input.contains(\'\\0\') {\n            detected_threats.push("null_byte".to_string());\n        }\n\n        // Check for control characters\n        for c in input.chars() {\n            if c.is_control() && c != \'\\n\' && c != \'\\r\' && c != \'\\t\' {\n                detected_threats.push("control_characters".to_string());\n                break;\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Check for unicode normalization issues\n        if self.has_suspicious_unicode(input) {\n            detected_threats.push("suspicious_unicode".to_string());\n        }\n\n        let valid = detected_threats.is_empty();\n        let sanitized_input = if valid {\n            Some(self.sanitize(input))\n        } else {\n            None\n        };\n\n        Ok(InputValidationResult {\n            valid,\n            reason: if valid { None } else { Some("Input validation failed".to_string()) },\n            threat_level: if valid { ThreatLevel::Info } else { ThreatLevel::Medium },\n            detected_threats,\n            sanitized_input,\n        })\n    }\n\n    /// Check for suspicious unicode\n    fn has_suspicious_unicode(&self, input: &str) -> bool {\n        for c in input.chars() {\n            // Check for zero-width characters\n            if c == \'\\u{200B}\' || c == \'\\u{200C}\' || c == \'\\u{200D}\' || c == \'\\u{FEFF}\' {\n                return true;\n            }\n            // Check for homoglyphs (simplified check)\n            if c > \'\\u{FFFF}\' && c.is_alphabetic() {\n                // Could be a homoglyph attack\n            }\n        }\n        false\n    }\n\n    /// Sanitize input\n    pub fn sanitize(&self, input: &str) -> String {\n        let mut sanitized = String::new();\n        \n        for c in input.chars() {\n            match c {\n                // Remove control characters except whitespace\n                c if c.is_control() && c != \'\\n\' && c != \'\\r\' && c != \'\\t\' => continue,\n                // Remove null bytes\n                \'\\0\' => continue,\n                // Escape HTML-like characters\n                \'<\' => sanitized.push_str("&lt;"),\n                \'>\' => sanitized.push_str("&gt;"),\n                \'&\' => sanitized.push_str("&amp;"),\n                \'"\' => sanitized.push_str("&quot;"),\n                \'\\\'\' => sanitized.push_str("&#x27;"),\n                // Keep other characters\n                c => sanitized.push(c),\n            }\n        }\n\n        sanitized\n    }\n}\n\nimpl Default for Rate Limiter\npub struct RateLimiter {\n    /// Request counts per client\n    counts: Arc<RwLock<HashMap<String, RateLimitEntry>>>,\n    /// Default limit per minute\n    default_limit: Self {\n        Self {\n            counts: Arc::new(RwLock::new(HashMap::new())),\n            default_limit: 60,\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Check if request is within rate limit\n    pub async fn check(&self, client_id: &str, _endpoint_id: &str) -> Result<bool> {\n        let mut counts = self.counts.write().await;\n        let now = Utc::now();\n        let window_start = now - chrono::Duration::seconds(60);\n\n        let entry = counts.entry(client_id.to_string()).or_insert(RateLimitEntry {\n            client_id: client_id.to_string(),\n            count: 0,\n            window_start: now,\n            limit: self.default_limit,\n        });\n\n        // Reset if window expired\n        if entry.window_start < window_start {\n            entry.count = 0;\n            entry.window_start = now;\n        }\n\n        entry.count += 1;\n        Ok(entry.count <= entry.limit)\n    }\n\n    /// Set custom limit for client\n    pub async fn set_limit(&self, client_id: &str, limit: u32) -> Result<()> {\n        let mut counts = self.counts.write().await;\n        if let Some(entry) = counts.get_mut(client_id) {\n            entry.limit = limit;\n        }\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Get remaining requests for client\n    pub async fn remaining(&self, client_id: &str) -> u32 {\n        let counts = self.counts.read().await;\n        if let Some(entry) = counts.get(client_id) {\n            entry.limit.saturating_sub(entry.count)\n        } else {\n            self.default_limit\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nimpl Default for RateLimiter {\n    fn default()    pub max_failed_requests: u32,\n    /// Maximum unique endpoints hit\n    pub max_unique_endpoints: u32,\n    /// Suspicious pattern threshold\n    pub suspicious_pattern_threshold: f32,\n}\n\nimpl       suspicious_pattern_threshold: 0.7,\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nimpl AbuseDetector {\n    /// Create new abuse detector\n    pub fn new() -> Self {\n        Self {\n            thresholds: = Vec::new();\n        let mut abuse_score = 0.0;\n\n        // Check request frequency\n        let requests_per_minute = self.calculate_requests_per_minute(request_log);\n        if requests_per_minute > self.thresholds.max_requests_per_minute {\n            indicators.push("high_request_frequency".to_string());\n            abuse_score += 0.3;\n        }\n\n        // Check for scanning behavior\n        let unique_endpoints = self.count_unique_endpoints(request_log);\n        if unique_endpoints > self.thresholds.max_unique_endpoints {\n            indicators.push("endpoint_scanning".to_string());\n            abuse_score += 0.2;\n        }\n\n        // Check for error harvesting\n        let failed_requests = request_log.iter().filter(|r| r.status_code >= 400).count();\n        if failed_requests > self.thresholds.max_failed_requests as usize {\n            indicators.push("error_harvesting".to_string());\n            abuse_score += 0.2;\n        }\n\n        // Check for timing patterns (automation)\n        if self.detect_automation(request_log) {\n            indicators.push("automated_requests".to_string());\n            abuse_score += 0.3;\n        }\n\n        Ok(AbuseDetectionResult {\n            detected: abuse_score >= self.thresholds.suspicious_pattern_threshold,\n            abuse_score,\n            indicators,\n            recommendation: if abuse_score > 0.5 {\n                "Consider blocking this client".to_string()\n            } else if abuse_score > 0.3 {\n                "Monitor this client closely".to_string()\n            } else {\n                String::new()\n            },\n        })\n    }\n\n    /// Calculate requests per minute\n    fn calculate_requests_per_minute(&self, request_log: &[APIRequest]) -> u32 {\n        if request_log.is_empty() {\n            return 0;\n        }\n        \n        let now = Utc::now();\n        let one_minute_ago = now - chrono::Duration::seconds(60);\n        \n        request_log.iter()\n            .filter(|r| r.timestamp > one_minute_ago)\n            .count() as u32\n    }\n\n    /// Count unique endpoints\n    fn count_unique_endpoints(&self, request_log: &[APIRequest]) -> u32 {\n        let endpoints: std::collections::HashSet<&str> = request_log.iter()\n            .map(|r| r.endpoint.as_str())\n            .collect();\n        endpoints.len() as u32\n    }\n\n    /// Detect automation patterns\n    fn detect_automation(&self, request_log: &[APIRequest]) -> bool {\n        if request_log.len() < 5 {\n            return false;\n        }\n\n        // Check for very consistent timing between requests\n        let intervals: Vec<i64> = request_log.windows(2)\n            .map(|w| (w[1].timestamp - w[0].timestamp).num_milliseconds())\n            .collect();\n\n        if intervals.is_empty() {\n            return false;\n        }\n\n        let mean = intervals.iter().sum::<i64>() as f64 / intervals.len() as f64;\n        let variance = intervals.iter()\n            .map(|i| (*i as f64 - mean).powi(2))\n            .sum::<f64>() / intervals.len() as f64;\n        let std_dev = variance.sqrt();\n\n        // Very low standard deviation indicates automation\n        std_dev < 50.0 // 50ms standard deviation\n    }\n}\n\nimpl Default for AbuseDetector {\n    fn default() -> Self {\n        Self::new()\n    }\n}\n\n/// API Request record\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct APIRequest {\n    /// Request    /// Model is being registered\n    Registering,\n    /// Model is registered and ready\n    Ready,\n    /// Model is deployed\n    Deployed,\n    /// Model is deprecated\n    Deprecated,\n    /// Model is archived\n    Archived,\n}\n\n/// Security scan result\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct SecurityScanResult {\n    /// Scan ID\n    pub scan_id: String,\n    /// Scan timestamp\n    pub scanned_at: DateTime<Utc>,\n    /// Vulnerabilities found\n    pub vulnerabilities: Vec<ModelVulnerability>,\n    /// Overall status\n    pub status: ScanStatus,\n    /// Recommendations\n    pub recommendations: Vec<String>,\n}\n\n/// Scan status\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n#[serde(rename_all = "snake_case")]\npub enum ScanStatus {\n    Passed,\n    Warning,\n    Failed,\n}\n\n/// Model provenance\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct ModelProvenance {\n    /// Model ID\n    pub model_id: String,\n    /// Training data sources\n    pub training_data: Vec<DataProvenance>,\n    /// Training configuration\n    pub training_config: HashMap<String, String>,\n    /// Parent models (if transfer learning)\n    pub parent_models: Vec<String>,\n    /// Transformations applied\n    pub transformations: Vec<String>,\n    /// Created by\n    pub created_by: String,\n    /// Created at\n    pub created_at: DateTime<Utc>,\n}\n\n/// Data provenance\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct DataProvenance {\n    /// Data source ID\n    pub source_id: String,\n    /// Source name\n    pub name: String,\n    /// Source location\n    pub location: String,\n    /// Data hash\n    pub hash: String,\n    /// Classification\n    pub classification: DataClassification,\n}\n\nimpl ModelRegistry {\n    /// Create new model registry\n    pub fn new() -> Self {\n        Self {\n            models: Arc::new(RwLock::new(HashMap::new())),\n            provenance: Arc::new(RwLock::new(HashMap::new())),\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Register a model\n    pub async fn register(&self, model: &AIModel) -> Result<ModelRegistrationResult> {\n        let registered = RegisteredModel {\n            model_id: model.id.clone(),\n            name: model.name.clone(),\n            version: model.version.clone(),\n            registered_at: Utc::now(),\n            status: ModelStatus::Ready,\n            security_scan: None,\n            tags: HashMap::new(),\n        };\n\n        let model_id = model.id.clone();\n        let mut models = self.models.write().await;\n        models.insert(model_id.clone(), registered);\n\n        // Create initial provenance\n        let prov = ModelProvenance {\n            model_id: model_id.clone(),\n            training_data: vec![],\n            training_config: HashMap::new(),\n            parent_models: vec![],\n            transformations: vec![],\n            created_by: "system".to_string(),\n            created_at: Utc::now(),\n        };\n        \n        let mut provenance = self.provenance.write().await;\n        provenance.insert(model_id, prov);\n\n        Ok(ModelRegistrationResult {\n            model_id: model.id.clone(),\n            status: ModelStatus::Ready,\n            registered_at: Utc::now(),\n        })\n    }\n\n    /// Get model provenance\n    pub async fn get_provenance(&self, model_id: &str) -> Result<Option<ModelProvenance>> {\n        let provenance = self.provenance.read().await;\n        Ok(provenance.get(model_id).cloned())\n    }\n\n    /// Update model status\n    pub async fn update_status(&self, model_id: &str, status: ModelStatus) -> Result<()> {\n        let mut models = self.models.write().await;\n        if let Some(model) = models.get_mut(model_id) {\n            model.status = status;\n        }\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Run security scan\n    pub async fn scan_model(&self, model_id: &str) -> Result<SecurityScanResult> {\n        let scan_result = SecurityScanResult {\n            scan_id: uuid::Uuid::new_v4().to_string(),\n            scanned_at: Utc::now(),\n            vulnerabilities: vec![],\n            status: ScanStatus::Passed,\n            recommendations: vec![],\n        };\n\n        let mut models = self.models.write().await;\n        if let Some(model) = models.get_mut(model_id) {\n            model.security_scan = Some(scan_result.clone());\n        }\n\n        Ok(scan_result)\n    }\n}\n\nimpl Default for ModelRegistry {\n    fn default() -> Self {\n        Self::new()\n    }\n}\n\n/// Model registration result\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct ModelRegistrationResult {\n    /// Model ID\n    pub model_id: String,\n    /// Status\n    pub status: ModelStatus,\n    /// Registration timestamp\n    pub registered_at: DateTime<Utc>,\n}\n\n/// Deployment Security\npub struct DeploymentSecurity {\n    /// Deployment configurations\n    deployments: Arc<RwLock<HashMap<String, DeploymentConfig>>>,\n}\n\n/// Deployment configuration\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct DeploymentConfig {\n    /// Deployment ID\n    pub deployment_id: String,\n    /// Model ID\n    pub model_id: String,\n    /// Environment\n    pub environment: DeploymentEnvironment,\n    /// Security controls\n    pub security_controls: Vec<String>,\n    /// Access policy\n    pub access_policy: DeploymentAccessPolicy,\n    /// Created at\n    pub created_at: DateTime<Utc>,\n}\n\n/// Deployment environment\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n#[serde(rename_all = "snake_case")]\npub enum DeploymentEnvironment {\n    Development,\n    Staging,\n    Production,\n}\n\n/// Deployment access policy\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct DeploymentAccessPolicy {\n    /// Require authentication\n    pub require_auth: bool,\n    /// Require mTLS\n    pub require_mtls: bool,\n    /// Allowed IP ranges\n    pub allowed_ips: Vec<String>,\n    /// Rate limit\n    pub rate_limit: u32,\n}\n\nimpl DeploymentSecurity {\n    /// Create new deployment security\n    pub fn new() -> Self {\n        Self {\n            deployments: Arc::new(RwLock::new(HashMap::new())),\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Secure endpoints\n    pub async fn secure(&self, endpoints: &[APIEndpoint]) -> Result<()> {\n        for endpoint in endpoints {\n            let config = DeploymentConfig {\n                deployment_id: endpoint.id.clone(),\n                model_id: String::new(),\n                environment: DeploymentEnvironment::Production,\n                security_controls: vec![\n                    "rate_limiting".to_string(),\n                    "input_validation".to_string(),\n                    "audit_logging".to_string(),\n                ],\n                access_policy: DeploymentAccessPolicy {\n                    require_auth: true,\n                    require_mtls: false,\n                    allowed_ips: vec![],\n                    rate_limit: 60,\n                },\n                created_at: Utc::now(),\n            };\n\n            let mut deployments = self.deployments.write().await;\n            deployments.insert(endpoint.id.clone(), config);\n        }\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Verify model for deployment\n    pub async fn verify_model(&self, model: &AIModel) -> Result<DeploymentVerificationResult> {\n        let mut checks = Vec::new();\n\n        // Check encryption\n        checks.push(DeploymentCheck {\n            name: "model_encryption".to_string(),\n            passed: model.encrypted,\n            message: if model.encrypted {\n                "Model is encrypted".to_string()\n            } else {\n                "Model is not encrypted".to_string()\n            },\n        });\n\n        // Check watermark\n        checks.push(DeploymentCheck {\n            name: "model_watermark".to_string(),\n            passed: model.watermarked,\n            message: if model.watermarked {\n                "Model is watermarked".to_string()\n            } else {\n                "Model is not watermarked".to_string()\n            },\n        });\n\n        // Check vulnerabilities\n        let vuln_count = model.vulnerabilities.len();\n        checks.push(DeploymentCheck {\n            name: "security_scan".to_string(),\n            passed: vuln_count == 0,\n            message: format!("{} vulnerabilities found", vuln_count),\n        });\n\n        let passed = checks.iter().all(|c| c.passed);\n\n        Ok(DeploymentVerificationResult {\n            model_id: model.id.clone(),\n            passed,\n            checks,\n            verified_at: Utc::now(),\n        })\n    }\n}\n\nimpl Default for DeploymentSecurity {\n    fn default() -> Self {\n        Self::new()\n    }\n}\n\n/// Deployment verification result\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct DeploymentVerificationResult {\n    /// Model ID\n    pub model_id: String,\n    /// Whether verification passed\n    pub passed: bool,\n    /// Individual checks\n    pub checks: Vec<DeploymentCheck>,\n    /// Verification timestamp\n    pub verified_at: DateTime<Utc>,\n}\n\n/// Individual deployment check\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct DeploymentCheck {\n    /// Check name\n    pub name: String,\n    /// Whether check passed\n    pub passed: bool,\n    /// Check message\n    pub message: String,\n}\n\n/// Audit Logger\npub struct AuditLogger {\n    /// Audit entries\n    entries: Arc<RwLock<Vec<MLOpsAuditEvent>>>,\n}\n\nimpl AuditLogger {\n    /// Create new audit logger\n    pub fn new() -> Self {\n        Self {\n            entries: Arc::new(RwLock::new(Vec::new())),\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Log an audit event\n    pub async fn log(&self, event: MLOpsAuditEvent) -> Result<()> {\n        let mut entries = self.entries.write().await;\n        entries.push(event);\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Get recent entries\n    pub async fn get_recent(&self, limit: usize) -> Vec<MLOpsAuditEvent> {\n        let entries = self.entries.read().await;\n        entries.iter().rev().take(limit).cloned().collect()\n    }\n}\n\nimpl Default for AuditLogger {\n    fn default() -> Self {\n        Self::new()\n    }\n}\n\n/// MLOps audit event\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct MLOpsAuditEvent {\n    /// Event ID\n    pub id: String,\n    /// Event type\n    pub event_type: MLOpsEventType,\n    /// System ID\n    pub system_id: Option<String>,\n    /// Model ID\n    pub model_id: Option<String>,\n    /// Pipeline ID\n    pub pipeline_id: String>,\n}\n\n/// MLOps event type\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n#[serde(rename_all = "snake_case")]\npub enum MLOpsEventType {\n    SystemSecured,\n    ModelRegistered,\n    ModelDeployed,\n    PipelineSecured,\n    AccessGranted,\n    AccessDenied,\n    SecurityScanCompleted,\n    VulnerabilityDetected,\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use
